  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f95881ff-22f1-4b45-acdc-926255a1487d'
      });
    }

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer13237498999267134855">前世的魏無羨萬人唾罵，聲名狼藉。<br/>嘔心瀝血護持師弟，<br/>師弟帶人端了他老巢，親自送他下地，<br/>縱橫一世，死無全屍。<br/>被鎮壓數年，<br/>曾興風作浪的一代魔道祖師，重生成了一個……<br/>腦殘。<br/>還特麼是個人人喊打的斷袖腦殘！<br/>我見諸君多有病，料諸君見我應如是。<br/>他決定敬業地做好一名腦殘。<br/>但修鬼道不修仙，任你千軍萬馬，十方惡霸，九州奇俠，高嶺之花，<br/>但凡化為一抔黃土，統統收歸旗下，為我所用，供我驅策！<br/>高貴冷豔悶騷攻×邪魅狂狷風騷受。<br/><br/><br/>As the grandmaster who founded demonic cultivation, Wei WuXian roamed the world in his wanton ways, hated by millions for the chaos he created. In the end, he was backstabbed b</span>
  <span id="freeText13237498999267134855" style="display:none">前世的魏無羨萬人唾罵，聲名狼藉。<br />嘔心瀝血護持師弟，<br />師弟帶人端了他老巢，親自送他下地，<br />縱橫一世，死無全屍。<br />被鎮壓數年，<br />曾興風作浪的一代魔道祖師，重生成了一個……<br />腦殘。<br />還特麼是個人人喊打的斷袖腦殘！<br />我見諸君多有病，料諸君見我應如是。<br />他決定敬業地做好一名腦殘。<br />但修鬼道不修仙，任你千軍萬馬，十方惡霸，九州奇俠，高嶺之花，<br />但凡化為一抔黃土，統統收歸旗下，為我所用，供我驅策！<br />高貴冷豔悶騷攻×邪魅狂狷風騷受。<br /><br /><br />As the grandmaster who founded demonic cultivation, Wei WuXian roamed the world in his wanton ways, hated by millions for the chaos he created. In the end, he was backstabbed by his dearest shidi and killed by powerful clans that combined to overpower him.<br /><br />He incarnates into the body of a lunatic who was abandoned by his clan and is later, unwillingly, taken away by a famous cultivator among the sects—Lan WangJi, his archenemy.<br /><br />This marks the start of a thrilling yet hilarious journey of attacking monsters, solving mysteries, and raising children. From the mutual flirtation along the way, Wei WuXian slowly realizes that Lan WangJi, a seemingly haughty and indifferent poker-face, holds more feelings for Wei WuXian than he is letting on…</span>

        if (this.up('#box')) {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function(i){i.setStyle({zIndex: $('box').getStyle('z-index')})});

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('edition_41832344').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
          $$('div.prototip').each(function (e) {
            if ($('edition_41832344').hasClassName('ignored')) {
              e.setStyle({'display': 'none'});
              return;
            }
            e.setStyle({'overflow': 'visible'});
          });

<div id="review_2557748801" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2557748801" />
    <a title="Kat" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4903141-kat"><img alt="Kat" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1444987369p2/4903141.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2557748801?book_show_action=true">Oct 23, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kat" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kat" href="/user/show/4903141-kat">Kat</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/42190679-grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4903141-kat?shelf=chinese-novels">chinese-novels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4903141-kat?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4903141-kat?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2557748801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10208810319572398209">This is one of the best translated c-novels out there. Exiled Rebels' translation quality is excellent. And the book itself, is a holy wow. <br/><br/>Before anything, this novel is categorized as BL, or boy love. So yes there is a gay romance. But don't let that stop you from reading this masterpiece. This novel is 10% super slowly hinted romance (the best kind), 10% complex relationships with side characters, and 80% killing demons and solving mysteries. It's basically an epic adventure. The character de</span>
  <span id="freeText10208810319572398209" style="display:none">This is one of the best translated c-novels out there. Exiled Rebels' translation quality is excellent. And the book itself, is a holy wow. <br /><br />Before anything, this novel is categorized as BL, or boy love. So yes there is a gay romance. But don't let that stop you from reading this masterpiece. This novel is 10% super slowly hinted romance (the best kind), 10% complex relationships with side characters, and 80% killing demons and solving mysteries. It's basically an epic adventure. The character development and pacing is extremely well done. I just finished reading 74 translated chapters, and I am now in book hangover territory. The novel is still being translated, one chapter a week.<br /><br />The main character is Wei Wuxian. He is a troublemaker with good intentions. He is shameless, mischievous, reckless and an arrogant super genius. He single-handedly started demonic cultivation. During the sunshot campaign, he used his dark powers to fight against tyranny and oppression, thus earning him a legendary reputation. After the war, people feared and misunderstood him. Eventually, the dark path took a toll on his temperament. Wei Wuxian got out of control, was betrayed and was killed. <br /><br />13 years later, Wei Wuxian is summoned into the body of a gay lunatic. The deal is that he gets to possess the lunatic's body for life, but he has to fulfill the original owner of the body's revenge wish. Along with that, he is also hiding his real identity because a lot of people hate/fear him for the demonic things he did in the past. Somewhere along the way, common goals align and he goes on a journey/adventure with Lan Wangji, an old friend from the past, who helps him hide his identity and stays by his side. Lan Wangji is very prim and proper, he is a stickler for rules, and the silent type. He has mastered the art of poker face and doesn’t show his emotions. Both men are badasses and there are a lot of hilarious interactions between the two of them. <br /><br />I also liked reading about the flashbacks of the past, showing us how the characters met, Wei Wuxian's relationships with side characters (like the backstory with his sworn brother Jiang Cheng) and how Wei Wuxian turned to the dark arts and became the infamous grandmaster. <br /><br />This book will take a while to get into. The first few chapters are really heavy with world building and character introduction. What's more, each character has three names - a birth name, a more formal name and a title. There are also a lot of different sects, with each character belonging to a certain sect. So that took a while to get used to. But once I got past all those important details, the story got better and better. Trust me. <br /><br />If you like action and adventure, slow-burn romance, paranormal mysteries, humor, well-developed characters, ancient fantasy world settings, then this is for you. <br /><br />The donghua (chinese anime) is also one of the best I’ve ever watched. I recommend everyone to watch the donghua after reading a few chapters of the novel. The donghua is on WeTV: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://wetv.vip/en/play/r8t02fkxr9jyvvn/e0029bmqymw">https://wetv.vip/en/play/r8t02fkxr9jy...</a><br /><br />UPDATE: Because a lot of people keep asking in the comments, the English translation is here: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://exiledrebelsscanlations.com/novels/grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation/">https://exiledrebelsscanlations.com/n...</a><br /><br />Also, there is a now Netflix TV series based on this novel called The Untamed, and it rocked big time.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10208810319572398209" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3233453935" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1786598342464521921">AFTER 520k WORDS, 113 CHAPTERS, 3 MONTHS AND THE LONGEST ANGSTY SLOWBURN EVER, I HAVE FINISHED MO DAO ZU SHIIIIIIIIII <i>*cries* </i><br/><br/>what do I do now<br/><br/>It's been an experience, really. Watching the dongua adaption, watching live action adaption (<i>would recommend watching an adaption before starting the book actually, as it helps one get a better sense of the characters/the character's multiple names and titles - the live action version 'the untamed' is on netflix</i>), reading the manhua and then finally finis</span>
  <span id="freeText1786598342464521921" style="display:none">AFTER 520k WORDS, 113 CHAPTERS, 3 MONTHS AND THE LONGEST ANGSTY SLOWBURN EVER, I HAVE FINISHED MO DAO ZU SHIIIIIIIIII <i>*cries* </i><br /><br />what do I do now<br /><br />It's been an experience, really. Watching the dongua adaption, watching live action adaption (<i>would recommend watching an adaption before starting the book actually, as it helps one get a better sense of the characters/the character's multiple names and titles - the live action version 'the untamed' is on netflix</i>), reading the manhua and then finally finishing the novel. The level of creativity the fans have in this fandom is also no joke - the art is incredible and the fanfic is top-tier. <s>I have an entire dedicated internet folder, if you ever want recs just hmu &gt;:)</s><br /><br />I think I want to write an entire post/review with my thoughts later on (especially because I loved the themes/tropes, including 'doing what you think is right even if everyone is against you'/the antihero arc/the slowburn/the juniors with one shared braincell, but had some other quibbles - like the narrative voice and lack of female characters, which is fixed a bit in the live action adaption) but for now I'll leave it here.<br /><br />but hey @ whoever recommended MDZS to me, you really introduced me to something awesome. I plan to float through the blissful land of the MDZS fandom for eternity. I only exist here now. Job? Friends? What are they. I only know wangxian.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1786598342464521921" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2701016127" />
    <a title="Xia Xia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/76171040-xia-xia"><img alt="Xia Xia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1515406366p2/76171040.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2701016127?book_show_action=true">Oct 24, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Xia Xia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Xia Xia" href="/user/show/76171040-xia-xia">Xia Xia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/42190679-grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation">review of another edition</a>

            Shelves:

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76171040-xia-xia?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76171040-xia-xia?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76171040-xia-xia?shelf=action">action</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/76171040-xia-xia?shelf=danmei">danmei</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2701016127" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9529342383967120350">Okay, let's face it. <br/>I cannot possibility give MDZS 5 stars from a literary perspective and it breaks my heart I need to remove 1 star for the following:<br/>1. Omniscient narrator with too much telling. I am being told the thoughts, emotions and characters' reasons for acting in one way or another<br/>2. Too many flashbacks sneaking up on the reader at the wrong time e.g as the MCs are about to have sex.<br/>3. An ending that was too subtle for my tastes (but the ending was compensated by the 14 extras availa</span>
  <span id="freeText9529342383967120350" style="display:none">Okay, let's face it. <br>I cannot possibility give MDZS 5 stars from a literary perspective and it breaks my heart I need to remove 1 star for the following:<br>1. Omniscient narrator with too much telling. I am being told the thoughts, emotions and characters' reasons for acting in one way or another<br>2. Too many flashbacks sneaking up on the reader at the wrong time e.g as the MCs are about to have sex.<br>3. An ending that was too subtle for my tastes (but the ending was compensated by the 14 extras available, so hey ho)<br><br><b> However! </b><br><br>This 520,000 words book has dominated my life for the past month.<br><br>It's one of the best xianxia (Chinese martial arts fantasy) I HAVE EVER READ.<br><br>Lan WangJi and Wei WuXian will forever hold a spot in my heart.<br><br>There is no official Chinese- English translation. The heroes are the voluntary fan translators that have spent 2 years of their lives to translate this book without requesting anything in return.<br><br>Worldbuilding - a thousand stars<br><br>Character development - The development of the MCs is just WOW! Also there is a huge array of supporting characters, each with impressive backgrounds and developmental arcs. I have fallen in love with all of them, even the villains. <br><br>Music, music, music!<br><br>Chinese Daoist Philosophy.<br><br>The hype over this book is real.<br><br>I don't know if this is a book for the MM Romance community. But if you love danmei or yaoi and are already familiar with the Chinese xianxia genre, I highly recommend it. <br><br>In my heart of hearts this book is 5 stars.<br><br>A low bow for our beautiful boys:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1571942350ra/28345884.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="9529342383967120350" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2966010607" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2966010607" />
    <a title="Sherwood Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/162084-sherwood-smith"><img alt="Sherwood Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1543007644p2/162084.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2966010607?book_show_action=true">Sep 05, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sherwood Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sherwood Smith" href="/user/show/162084-sherwood-smith">Sherwood Smith</a>
      </span>

          added it


          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/42190679-grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/162084-sherwood-smith?shelf=wuxi-xianxia">wuxi-xianxia</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2966010607" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4337885105166902946">Curious about the novel behind the series <i>The Untamed</i>, which series turns out is faithful to the novel, good and not so good.<br/><br/>The translation into English is full of errors in spelling, grammar, and proper use of actual English words, but it was done by an unpaid volunteer out of generosity, so readers who get poked out of the reading experience by that sort of thing should know that going in, be prepared, and be grateful at least there's a translation.<br/><br/>The plot is bent around BL, so don't look fo</span>
  <span id="freeText4337885105166902946" style="display:none">Curious about the novel behind the series <i>The Untamed</i>, which series turns out is faithful to the novel, good and not so good.<br /><br />The translation into English is full of errors in spelling, grammar, and proper use of actual English words, but it was done by an unpaid volunteer out of generosity, so readers who get poked out of the reading experience by that sort of thing should know that going in, be prepared, and be grateful at least there's a translation.<br /><br />The plot is bent around BL, so don't look for rational logic behind character motivations; there are very few. Most of the plot decisions are manipulated toward maximum angst and hurt/comfort for the leads, whose emotional state often reads adolescent female-gaze. But given that framework, there are some interesting characters, some genuinely comic scenes, and plenty of action between long confessional and comfort scenes.<br /><br />For English readers peering through the tiny keyhole at the vast world of female-written Chinese novels (some of which get millions of hits in their first week of publication) this appears to be a solid, entertaining example of BL--which is deeply subversive considering the government's attempt to control any hint of homoerotic material in the media world.<br /><br />Go, girls, go!</span>
  <a data-text-id="4337885105166902946" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

<div id="review_2594814190" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2594814190" />
    <a title="Yeyu" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11894891-yeyu"><img alt="Yeyu" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1442658714p2/11894891.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2594814190?book_show_action=true">Nov 14, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Yeyu" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Yeyu" href="/user/show/11894891-yeyu">Yeyu</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=chinese">chinese</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=bl">bl</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=hate-this-dynamic">hate-this-dynamic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=meh">meh</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11894891-yeyu?shelf=squicky">squicky</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2594814190" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16352211409950449702">Interesting to see this also so hyped on goodreads. I actually rated it 3 stars on saowen since that was the threshold for just ok on that platform, but 2 stars here as it represents just ok on goodreads.<br/><br/>My review is strictly based on the Chinese version and not the translation nor any other adaptions.<br/><br/><b>Pros: </b><br/><br/>- Good pacing that keeps you reading and entertained, despite the predictable plot. There were definitely flaws, but it was entertaining enough for me to disregard them. Perhaps I was not inv</span>
  <span id="freeText16352211409950449702" style="display:none">Interesting to see this also so hyped on goodreads. I actually rated it 3 stars on saowen since that was the threshold for just ok on that platform, but 2 stars here as it represents just ok on goodreads.<br /><br />My review is strictly based on the Chinese version and not the translation nor any other adaptions.<br /><br /><b>Pros: </b><br /><br />- Good pacing that keeps you reading and entertained, despite the predictable plot. There were definitely flaws, but it was entertaining enough for me to disregard them. Perhaps I was not invested enough to care about any loose ends since I forgot most of what I read.<br /><br />- Passable prose<br /><br />- Humorous to an extent. At least the humor was less annoying than the author's other popular work<br /><br />- Much of the cons come as an aftertaste of fridge logic<br /><br /><br /><b>Not my cuppa/Personal Squicks: </b><br /><br />- Appeals to mainstream tastes, specifically the dynamics of a taciturn, mysterious stoic LI top and a noisy, saintly OP (self-insert) MC bottom<br /><br />- Overall MC is not Moe for me, which reduces my enjoyment. As a reader I am primarily motivated by how Moe I find the bottom. <br /><br />- Scenes with LI/top getting drunk were not the result of Gap Moe, just awkward AF.<br /><br />- Often miscategorized (imho) as Xiuzhen/Xiuxian genre, when there is no one training for immortality except for perhaps the MC's master. Usually Xiuzhen has a focus on man vs fate/nature (gaining immortality goes against nature), often ultimately becoming man vs gods/Heaven/demons, whereas no such conflict is present in this story. No one in this fic seems to really care about immortality, and the scope of the setting is limited without involving other planes of existence (which is a defining feature of the Xiuzhen genre). At best I think this should be categorized as Xianxia genre. There is magic which does use generic Xiuzhen cultivation system, but the plot revolves around very mortal affairs and soap opera conflict.<br /><br />- Maybe I'm just too old for this<br /><br /><br /><b>Cons:</b><br /><br />- Juvenile characters and dialogue. Specifically, teenagers (younger gen) feel like kindergarten children, while adults act/talk/think like teenage girls from junior high. With a serious case of Chuunibyou. Lots of screaming, OTT hysterics. Many side characters seem to have below-average IQ/EQ. I would not have been as annoyed if the fic was super light-hearted and not meant to be taken seriously, but despite the humor, it seems the fic is somewhat meant to be taken seriously. At least there is a very zealous group of fans who take this fic <i>really</i> seriously.<br /><br />- MC is right no matter what. People who don't agree with the MC just don't understand how ~selfless~ and ~good~ the saintly MC is, even though MC pretty much acts without considering any negative consequences others must endure thanks to his impulsive heroics. To me it is kinda problematic if the MC's (less severe) problems are shown as always more important/severe than other people's problems. MC is portrayed as a victim and others are shown wronging him for wanting him to take responsibility for something he is mostly responsible for (there was this one dude who always went into hysterics which does not help his case, as it decreases reader sympathy toward the dude and makes readers more sympathetic to MC). Woe is the MC...people just do not understand how holy and selfless his self-righteous intentions were, but as Jesus he will keep his reasons to himself and still save these poor fools, even if they are thankless.... Um... yeah, I'm very uncomfortable with a shallow worldview where everything revolves around the MC, so this is not a story worth re-reading for me. I mostly ignored these issues when I read for the first time because I was more interested in the story.<br /><br />- Some antagonists are so idiotic it's difficult to feel conflict tension due to how pathetic they are. Same goes to the pedestrian opposition--I remember feeling quite frustrated at how stupid and immature they are, instead of feeling sympathy for the MC as the author might have intended.<br /><br />Don't get me wrong, I was entertained and did enjoy the story, reading everything in practically one sitting even while I was squicked by several issues. I can see why the story is popular, but I can't say it's a shining example of what the Chinese BL community has to offer.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16352211409950449702" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm going to re-read this amazing book soon, that's for sure. I'll also read the other books by this extremely talented author. This is highly recommended you guys, please give this story and these </span>

I can't begin to describe how much I love Wei WuXian, he's so adorable, brave and selfless. He and Lan Zhan are my ultimate OTP. Even the extra chapters were as engaging as the main plot. I'm going to re-read this amazing book soon, that's for sure. I'll also read the other books by this extremely talented author. This is highly recommended you guys, please give this story and these amazing characters a chance to bring more joy to your lives ❤️❤️❤️.</span>

<div id="review_3208118768" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3208118768" />
    <a title="Leo 飛べ" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42979517-leo"><img alt="Leo 飛べ" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1595862709p2/42979517.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3208118768?book_show_action=true">Feb 26, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Leo 飛べ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Leo 飛べ" href="/user/show/42979517-leo">Leo 飛べ</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title=" " href="/book/show/42190679-grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42979517-leo?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42979517-leo?shelf=diverse-lit">diverse-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42979517-leo?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/42979517-leo?shelf=2020">2020</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3208118768" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3688969350627522235"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>What he hadn’t expected was that when everyone feared him and flattered him, Lan WangJi scolded him right in his face; when everyone spurned him and loathed him, Lan WangJi stood by his side..</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><b>Actual rating: 2.75★</b><br/><br/>I did it. I read this monster of a book and survived the process. <br/><br/><b>Mo Dao Zu Shi</b> is a <a href='https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xianxia_novel' rel='nofollow noopener'>xianxia</a> webnovel that has kindly been fan translated by <a href='https://exiledrebelsscanlations.com/novels/grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Exiled Rebel Scans</a>.<br/><br/>I never thought I'd be interested in reading this book if <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2950001000?book_show_action=true&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Silvia</a> hadn't filled my Twitter timeline with fanarts of W</span>
  <span id="freeText3688969350627522235" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>What he hadn’t expected was that when everyone feared him and flattered him, Lan WangJi scolded him right in his face; when everyone spurned him and loathed him, Lan WangJi stood by his side..</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br /><br /><b>Actual rating: 2.75★</b><br /><br />I did it. I read this monster of a book and survived the process. <br /><br /><b>Mo Dao Zu Shi</b> is a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Xianxia_novel" rel="nofollow noopener">xianxia</a> webnovel that has kindly been fan translated by <a href="https://exiledrebelsscanlations.com/novels/grandmaster-of-demonic-cultivation/" rel="nofollow noopener">Exiled Rebel Scans</a>.<br /><br />I never thought I'd be interested in reading this book if <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2950001000?book_show_action=true&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Silvia</a> hadn't filled my Twitter timeline with fanarts of Wei WuXian and Lan WangJi. But in spite of having enjoyed my time with these characters, I still have to say I found the novel to be definitely overhyped, furthermore, contrary to a lot of fans, I think the manhua (the comic version) is superior to the original novel itself. Some might argue that the reason behind this lays in the syntactic and grammatical errors I found throughout the text—it <i>is</i> a fan translation after all, and I am a little obsessed with grammar— or the frequent flashbacks, which often appeared out of nowhere leaving me confused and annoyed for pages and pages, whereas the manhua eases the reader into said flashbacks (but I guess it's easier when you add the visual impact to it all). <br /><br />Despite my stylistic and grammatical issues, what made me decide to lower the rating for this book is the homophobia—which is weird and disappointing seeing as the endgame romance in this book is between two men. I understand Chinese culture is different, and that in China there's a heavy censorship therefore people have less access to queer content and overall less awareness about certain issues, however what I can't, and won't, justify is seeing <b>a gay man being associated with predatory behaviour multiple times</b>, as well as the MC taking advantage of said predatory stereotype for the first 10 or so chapters of the novel. I almost <b>DNFed</b> the book because of it, so if it's something that triggers or bothers you, please think of yourself first and skip this one. <br /><br />What I <i>did</i> like about this book was the world the author created: it's complex, and crafted with extreme care to details. I loved learning about the different Clans/Sects and their traditions, especially as everything is filled with Chinese mythology and philosophy. And, of course, I also enjoyed the slow burn romance between stoic Lan WangJi and disaster demiro-bisexual* Wei WuXian: it was heartwarming to read and to witness. <br /><i>*It's not said in the novel, but I sort of understood it from the way Wei WuXian acted. Please do not consider this as representation.</i><br /><br />Overall while I did enjoy parts of this book, the comedy had me laugh and the world had my jaw drop, I also felt extremely underwhelmed. I'd say give MDZS a go if you want to try something new, or you want to dive into a non-Eurocentric fantasy novel. Do check out the trigger warnings down below though, and maybe read Silvia's <a href="https://silviareadsbooks.wordpress.com/2019/09/23/so-you-want-to-get-into-mo-dao-zu-shi-mdzs-the-untamed/" rel="nofollow noopener">guide</a> on how to best dive into MDZS. Otherwise, if you're interested in the story, you can also watch <b>The Untamed</b> or read the manhua. <br /><br /><br /><b>Content and Trigger warnings for</b>: <i>predatory depiction of queer (mostly gay) men, incest, violence, homophobia, corpse mutilation, misogyny, grief, mass murder, death of a loved one, alcohol, questionable consent, abuse.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3688969350627522235" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3405001814" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3405001814" />
    <a title="Arunima" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27283906-arunima"><img alt="Arunima" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1598720527p2/27283906.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3405001814?book_show_action=true">Jun 22, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Arunima" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Arunima" href="/user/show/27283906-arunima">Arunima</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=2020-reads">2020-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=aty-challenge-2020">aty-challenge-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=popsugar-challenge-2020">popsugar-challenge-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=mm-romance">mm-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=lgbtq">lgbtq</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=historical-romance">historical-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=translated-works">translated-works</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27283906-arunima?shelf=historic-fictions">historic-fictions</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3405001814" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13522880240338323498"><br/><b> *Read under POPSUGAR READING CHALLENGE 2020 for - <i> A book written by an author in their 20s </i>* </b> and also <b> under *Around The Year in 52 Books Challenge 2020 for - <i> A book by an author whose real name you are not quite sure how to pronounce. </i>* </b><br/><br/><b> Mo Dao Zu Shi offered a wonderful story, complex but equally wonderful characters, and the most amazing romance. </b> It's a Chinese novel translated by Exel Rebels Scanlations on their website. It doesn't have an official translated print so that's the only pl</span>
  <span id="freeText13522880240338323498" style="display:none"><br /><b> *Read under POPSUGAR READING CHALLENGE 2020 for - <i> A book written by an author in their 20s </i>* </b> and also <b> under *Around The Year in 52 Books Challenge 2020 for - <i> A book by an author whose real name you are not quite sure how to pronounce. </i>* </b><br /><br /><b> Mo Dao Zu Shi offered a wonderful story, complex but equally wonderful characters, and the most amazing romance. </b> It's a Chinese novel translated by Exel Rebels Scanlations on their website. It doesn't have an official translated print so that's the only place you can read it. I came across the book's manhua and I was really enjoying but I was super confused, because mark my words, <i> the story is pretty heavy. </i> It's too heavy for a manga. A manga can't depict the entire story, the details, and everything else that's going on. While it was a nice, visual representation of this wonderful story, I wouldn't recommend it reading before the book. SO I myself dropped the manga and switched to the translated book.<br /><br />Now, about the translation. It's a pretty good translation. I quite enjoyed it. But despite it being a decent translation, you know the entire time that what you're reading is a translated work, not the actual thing. So sometimes, it just feels off. But it didn't bother me that much. I was really enjoying the story and the characters and of course the lovely gay romance. <br /><br /><i> <b> The romance is top-notch. </b> </i> <br />It's a <b> super slow burn. </b> Just the way I wanted it to be. While the anime and manga are censored quite a bit, the book's pretty explicit when it has to be, so I was glad about that. I love the chemistry between the characters. Wei Wuxian with his dense, oblivious playful charisma and Lan Wangji with his super cold, impassive demeanor. But also, at the same time, it's so endearing to see that underneath all that stone-faced beauty, he is just a lovely cinnamon roll, hopelessly in love with the densest man on the face of this earth. I sympathized with him so much, lol. <br /><br />The story was great, so was the romance. I am really thankful for the scanlation group for translating the book so wonderfully. It must have been a lot of work because that's a think ass novel. Honestly, it's super long and the chapters are pretty long as well. There were quite a few editing errors here and there, and sometimes the writing didn't sit with me that's why I can't give it any more stars. Though I really, really appreciate the time and effort that has been put into the translation. I really enjoyed reading this and I completely get the reason behind the <i> huuuuge </i> fanbase of Mo Dao Zu Shi. I will definitely try some of the author's other works sometime.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13522880240338323498" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2957718735" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2957718735" />
    <a title="emma" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/42163117-emma"><img alt="emma" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508217767p2/42163117.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

<span id="freeTextContainer14823421610556775758">☆ no rating ☆<br/><br/>this was a very self-indulgent read because i love my oblivious cultivators, but i'd recommend starting out with one of the adaptations. this is pretty long and can be a bit dense since it's a translation and sometimes the switch between timelines isn't obviously marked. there were also a couple of scenes with dubious consent. <br/><br/>overall this was a good time and it made me really happy to spend time with these characters again <3<br/><br/>(Jin Zixuan still has no rights and Yanli deserved better</span>
  <span id="freeText14823421610556775758" style="display:none">☆ no rating ☆<br /><br />this was a very self-indulgent read because i love my oblivious cultivators, but i'd recommend starting out with one of the adaptations. this is pretty long and can be a bit dense since it's a translation and sometimes the switch between timelines isn't obviously marked. there were also a couple of scenes with dubious consent. <br /><br />overall this was a good time and it made me really happy to spend time with these characters again &lt;3<br /><br />(Jin Zixuan still has no rights and Yanli deserved better)<br /><br /><a href="https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCE1kZZ4FraiQm5rO0KMaD0w" rel="nofollow noopener">Youtube</a> ☆ <a href="https://twitter.com/maelysreads" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2882771248" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14882613326954561254"><b>5 <i>completely addicted as fuck to this book for perhaps my entire fucking life at this point</i> stars</b><br/><br/>Here’s a very short summary of why I adore this book so much:<br/><br/>1. <b>Wei Ying and Lan Zhan:</b> I just adore how on the surface you can’t get two people anymore different from each other, but then the moment you peel off the first cover you realize that they are the exact same person. They share the same morality, view and respect for people, one single brain cell, sense of sacrifice, and crazy ass love for t</span>
  <span id="freeText14882613326954561254" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>completely addicted as fuck to this book for perhaps my entire fucking life at this point</i> stars</b><br /><br />Here’s a very short summary of why I adore this book so much:<br /><br />1. <b>Wei Ying and Lan Zhan:</b> I just adore how on the surface you can’t get two people anymore different from each other, but then the moment you peel off the first cover you realize that they are the exact same person. They share the same morality, view and respect for people, one single brain cell, sense of sacrifice, and crazy ass love for the other. *cries at the sheer perfection*<br />2. <b>An incredibly huge assortment of very well built characters:</b> Ahh.. I think this just says it all. The character tray is crazy, and the way the author has taken care to give almost everyone at least some compelling backstory is to put it into one word- brilliant.<br />3.<b> ANGST. Angst. and. A-N-G-S-T:</b> Look guys, you have one person who died a horrible death due to political manipulation and misunderstandings, and the other who waited 13 years in a world that treated the love of his life like trash without knowing if he would ever see him again, and that is just the beginning.<br />4.<b> Excellent depictions of political ideologies.</b> Urgh, this post is long enough already, so I won’t say much more.<br />5.<b> How every single character acts as a foil to another:</b> Again another thing that you need to read the book to understand.<br />6.<b> Look man, we have a guy who turned into a villain solely because Lan Zhan is too fucking pretty. Period.</b> And I just love how every other villain has a really strong moral/circumstantial reason for their acts of villainy, and then there’s this guy.<br />7.<b> The confession scene:</b> *chefs kiss* ‘nough said.<br />8.<b> WangXian and rabbits.</b> You will get this if you read the book.<br /><br />You can read my entire fangirling on my blog <b>
  <a href="https://readingunderstreetlamps.wordpress.com/2019/11/11/mo-dao-zu-shi-mo-xiang-tong-xiu/" rel="nofollow noopener">here</a>
</b>.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('TbjEjJ0iNDL39QFzgpNHIasoTTBpTZniVA18vx857iVMxVrxCLmFKgRs7Yb2K75NYVwFx1tPqKMGPvGJKT67zQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('R8MT7BwQgb9pwvGUkL5cz7cYNh7P2w0gWkmEWD06xAdGvo2RiYswp5pbHWHkBqWjfWx+6f3ZPGEIegluCz2R7w==')})
  }
